Various Agencies Meet to Prevent Cholera 146

Eleventh Designated as Propaganda Day

The Cholera Prevention and Injection Propaganda Committee, jointly organized by the municipal party and government agencies, held its first meeting the day before yesterday. More than ten committee members from the Municipal Party Department, Society, Public Security, Education, Public Works, and Health Bureau, including Shen Gao, Chen Ming, and Chen Lengseng, were present. Chairman Shen Gao resolved (1) to designate May 11th as Cholera Prevention Propaganda Day. On this day, all agencies and organizations must effectively publicize the simple methods of cholera prevention and the benefits of preventing infection after injection; (2) to assign responsibilities to various groups to promote charitable organizations, factories, businesses, the Social Bureau, shantytowns, the Public Security Bureau, schools, the Education Bureau, transportation undertakings, the Public Works Bureau, party, government, military, and police groups, the Municipal Party Department, and the Public Security Bureau. The above groups are all handled in coordination with the Health Bureau; (3) to designate every fourth Thursday of the month at 1:00 PM as the date for the regular meetings of this committee. If there are temporary matters that need to be discussed, the committee may issue a letter to convene a meeting on a fixed date; (4) to pass fourteen items of the expanded method for Cholera Prevention to assign promotional supervision and implementation.

Shangyifang Tenants 147

Appeal to Landlord Shanshan Hall 148

The tenants of Shangyifang in the French Concession's Baxianqiao have appealed to the landlord, Shanshan Hall, for relief, as the landlord Shangyi Company rented land to build houses and arbitrarily increased rents. They previously requested a rent reduction but received no satisfactory response. Therefore, they prepared a letter to the landlord, Shanshan Hall, requesting relief. The letter reads: Respectfully, we have investigated that your esteemed hall has many properties in Baxianqiao and other places in the French Concession. The rents have always been very low, and the people are very grateful. Your esteemed hall embraces universal love and has always provided guidance and rescue to people, which has a vast and altruistic intent. We believe that you will provide relief to our oppressed tenants. We will now state the main points: Shangyifang, west of the Baxianqiao vegetable market, was originally rented by poor vendors. Last spring, your esteemed hall contracted with Shangyi Company to renovate and sublet the area, arbitrarily changing the name of the lane to Shangyifang and privately collecting tens of thousands of taels in rental fees. The monthly rent is five or six times higher than before. When the tenants paid the deposit, they hoped that the market would flourish and business would prosper, so they would temporarily endure the pain. Now, a new road has been opened north of the vegetable market, named Manyixing Road, but few pedestrians pass through this road. Moreover, business in the vegetable market has also greatly decreased compared to before. Therefore, the decline in business in Shangyifang is equal to that of the vegetable market. The tenants, seeing this situation, fear that it will become increasingly difficult to support themselves. Therefore, they requested Shangyi Company to reduce the rent and return the small rent to show consideration. However, Shangyi Company arbitrarily transferred the management rights to the Chinese Business Company in order to shirk responsibility. We believe that the land ownership belongs entirely to your esteemed hall. Now, Shangyi Company's actions violate the French Consul General's ban on subletting. We request your esteemed hall to conduct a detailed investigation and order the company to automatically reduce rents and return the small rents to appease the public and protect your reputation (omitted below). This is a request to Master Moss of Shanshan Hall.

Page 12

Red Cross Funds Relief for Shaanxi and Gansu

The Shaanxi Branch of the Chinese Red Cross recently received a telegram from Yang Hucheng, Chairman of the Shaanxi Provincial Government, stating that Shaanxi Province has suffered three years of drought, with people dying everywhere. The tragedy is unprecedented. The Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Executive Committee resolved to issue 8 million yuan in public bonds to aid the disaster victims, which was celebrated by everyone, hoping for rebirth. However, several months have passed and it has not been implemented. Hope is in sight, but the need for relief is even more urgent. After repeated appeals from all parties, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek fortunately approved the issuance of 500,000 yuan, which can temporarily alleviate the urgent need, but it is still a drop in the bucket. Recently, we received a telegram from our provincial relief committee's representative in Beijing, Meng Faqi, stating that there were rumors that 300,000 yuan of the aforementioned allocation would be reallocated to the four provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia. We were shocked and horrified to hear this, because just as the supply of food runs out and the disaster situation becomes more serious, if relief is not provided immediately, the entire remaining population of Shaanxi will have no chance of survival. In addition to directly telegraphing Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to order the original amount to be issued in order to maintain credibility, we respectfully telegraph you, pleading for your compassion for the heavy disaster in Shaanxi, and immediately telegraph the central government to investigate whether there is any agreement on the aforementioned reallocation and immediately cancel it to ensure that it is implemented to the end. We will be eternally grateful for your kindness. This is an urgent telegram. Sincerely, Yang Hucheng, Chairman of the Shaanxi Provincial Government.

The Gansu Branch of the Chinese Red Cross recently received a joint report from Huang Bingyi and Wu Jun, the heads of the Dangtu branch, Cai Junchuan and Shi Qingting, the heads of the Dangtu Caishi Buddhist Association, Yang Chucai, the former magistrate of Zhengning County in Gansu, and Yang Bingchen, the current principal of the First Middle School of Gansu, stating that Gansu is suffering from three disasters of heaven, earth, and man, which are actually worse than those in Shaanxi and Henan. Mr. Yang and others have been in Gansu for many years and have witnessed the suffering. Because there are very few people from Gansu traveling to Beijing and Shanghai, they cannot promote it as much as possible. Therefore, they have described the tragic situation they have seen and heard and prepared a report at their own expense, which has been forwarded by the Dangtu Red Cross branch. It is now disclosed here to clarify the true situation of the disaster in Gansu and to jointly plan for relief. The original text is divided into three items: (A) Drought: Gansu has suffered a drought for seventeen years, with hail disasters. The droughts in the eighteenth and nineteenth years were particularly severe. According to letters from friends in Gansu, there was no rain in October, and both the summer and autumn seasons in the nineteenth year yielded no harvest. In addition, the military food supply has been provided to the Northwest Army for many years, which is like adding salt to the wound. Two months ago, the price of grain in Lanzhou, the provincial capital, rose to 14 yuan per dou for wheat (the Gansu dou is large, one dou equals nine Su dou), 9 yuan per dou for millet seeds, and 10 yuan and more per dou for yellow rice. Recently, the price of wheat has risen to 23 or 24 yuan per dou, and about 30 yuan per 100 jin of wheat flour. The prices of other grains have also increased. Therefore, there are starving people everywhere, and corpses are everywhere. In Huining and Dingxi counties, people are eating human flesh, as reported in the Xin Shen and Shen Xin newspapers last year. According to reports from relief workers and people concerned, from the 17th year to the end of January of the 20th year, more than 2.3 million people died from freezing and starvation. It can be said to be a tragedy. (B) Earthquake: The earthquake in Longdong and Longnan counties in Gansu in the tenth year was unprecedented in the past hundred years. Cracks in the ground and landslides buried countless people and animals. According to calculations from Haiyuan, Qingshui, Zhengrong, Guyuan, and Longde counties, more than 30,000 people were buried. In total, it is estimated that more than 150,000 people were killed in the earthquake in various counties, with a property loss of more than 7 million yuan. In the sixteenth year, there was another major earthquake in Hexi, Wuwei, Pingfan, Gulang, Zhenfan, Yongchang, and other counties in Gansu. The houses in Wuwei Dongguan were destroyed and turned into flat ground. The houses and city walls in Gulang County all collapsed, and the county magistrate and prison officers were buried. After the earthquake in Wuwei, there was a flood that drowned more than 1,000 people. This is an unprecedented disaster that is unique to all provinces. (C) Man-made Disaster: After Feng Yuxiang's army entered Gansu in the fifteenth year, it incited a rebellion by the Gansu army led by Zhang Zhaojia and Huang Degui, which was not quelled until the sixteenth year. Although the number of deaths was not very high, the loss of property and the supply of grain were significant. Since the seventeenth year, Ma Zhongying and Ma Tingxian's rebellion has affected the overall situation, and there has been fighting between soldiers and bandits and revenge killings between Hui and Han people. Daohe, Didao, Ningding, Zhenfan, Pingfan, and other counties are the places where the Hui army has been active, burning and killing at will, turning them into scorched earth. Last year, 3,000 Han people were killed by Ma Tingxian's Hui army in Tianshui County, and the loss of property goes without saying. My nephew, Bingchen, recently returned to Suzhou from Gansu and described the disaster in detail, with tears in his eyes. Chu Cai has been in Gansu since the first year of Xuantong of the Qing Dynasty, serving four terms until he left Zhengning County in June of the seventeenth year and returned to his hometown, and he often communicates with people in Gansu, so he knows the situation in Gansu. Now, reading the newspapers, he has repeatedly seen reports of urgent relief efforts in Henan and Shaanxi, while Gansu is secondary. However, he does not know that the droughts, earthquakes, and man-made disasters in Gansu have come one after another and are unique to the country. The disaster is actually worse than those in Shaanxi and Henan. However, there are very few people from Gansu traveling to Beijing and Shanghai, so they cannot promote it as much as possible. Moreover, the roads are rugged, and bandits are rampant, so philanthropists are unwilling to go to investigate in person, which has resulted in the fact that thousands of people are dying in Gansu every day, which is the most tragic and unfair thing. Chu Cai humbly follows the Prime Minister's legacy and holds the goals of equality and the people's livelihood and has been in Gansu for many years and has witnessed the suffering, so he cannot help but plead for the people of Gansu. He earnestly implores your association to show universal compassion, order appropriate personnel to quickly bring huge sums of money to save the innocent victims, and this will be boundless merit. Cai has been a vegetarian for many years and will never lie. I sincerely hope that you will consider it and be grateful.

Shanghai Volunteer Corps Chinese Company Monthly Cup Shooting Competition 151

Slow Fire, Separate Targets

250 Yards, Two Bunkers

The 25th Shanghai Volunteer Corps Chinese Company Monthly Cup competition has already begun. The shooting competition is held from May each year to April of the following year, forming a session. A total of twelve shots are fired. The entire team is divided into five classes: Special, A, B, C, and D. Each class awards a cup to the shooter with the best score in each shooting session. Slow fire is used, with separate targets, at 250 yards and two bunkers. Five shots are fired at each bunker, with a maximum score of 50 points, to train physical fitness and improve shooting skills. It is reported that in this session, Wu Guanghua ranked first in the Special Class with 42 points, He Bingcheng ranked second with 39 points, and Xie Hong ranked third with 37 points. Zhang Qixiang ranked first in Class A with 38 points, Wu Shouwen ranked second with 38 points, and Zhang Naibin ranked third with 38 points. Xu Binkui ranked first in Class B with 37 points, Shi Binggui ranked second with 32 points, and Zhou Qingen ranked third with 30 points. Xu Dewen ranked first in Class C with 34 points, Huang Qixun ranked second with 34 points, and Ding Xibao ranked third with 31 points. Zhu Xi ranked first in Class D with 32 points, Zhou Weixin ranked second with 27 points, and Chu Qin Yun ranked third with 26 points. Cups are awarded according to regulations to encourage them.

Apprentice Beaten to Death by Colleagues 156

Zhou Xiqiao, 39 years old, from Dongchang Town, Qidong County, worked in the printing department of Liangchen Haoyou Society on Beijing Road. His son, Fusheng (an only son adopted by four families), is 15 years old this year. He was recommended by his brother to work as an apprentice in the Yiming Printing House opened by Lin Heqin at 15 Xinshun Lane, Gamsdong Road, French Concession, in July last year. On the 18th of last month, at 9:00 PM, Fusheng was working on the printing press, running the motor at full speed. His colleague Liu Wendao saw him playing ball nearby and, fearing danger, tried to stop him, but he did not listen. Another colleague, Wang Mujin (about 22 or 23 years old) from Jiangwan, slapped Zhou's face. Zhou fought back, and Wang used an iron key from the printing press to hit Zhou's head, kicking him several times. Zhou's left forehead was hit with a hole, and blood flowed like a stream. Colleagues took tooth powder to bandage him, but the blood continued to flow, and the injury became serious. Zhou's uncle and fellow villagers surrounded Wang Mujin and wanted to take him to the police station for investigation. However, Lin Dehua, the accountant of the printing house, came forward to mediate and guaranteed medical treatment and compensation. On the 24th, Fusheng was sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment. However, the injury became meningitis, and the treatment was ineffective. He died at 3:00 AM the day before yesterday. The murderer, Wang Mujin, learned that Fusheng's injury was serious and that he had died. He fled back to Jiangwan overnight with his father, Wang Maofu (father and son work together). The father of the deceased reported the incident to the police. The police sent detectives to arrest the murderer, but he was nowhere to be found. Only the iron key used in the crime was taken to the police station. The body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan branch hall for an autopsy. Yesterday, the Criminal Section of the French Police Department reported to the French Concession Hall. Judge Zhu Cheng examined the body and sat in the official position. According to the informant's report, the circumstances of the case were explained, and the murder weapon was presented. According to the father of the deceased's appeal to arrest the murderer and redress the grievance, Judge Zhu questioned the witness Liu Wendao about the circumstances of the incident. It was determined that Zhou Fusheng died before his death because he was hit in the head with an iron key by Wang Mujin and sent to the hospital for treatment. After a long time, the treatment was ineffective, and he died. The corpse was allowed to be collected by his family. The defendant's residence is in Jiangwan. The plaintiff should file a lawsuit for investigation and judgment.

Educational News

Important News

Hubei Province Promotes Compulsory Education 172

The Ministry of Education, according to the Hubei Education Department's submission of the Hubei Provincial Compulsory Education First Phase Implementation Plan and the 19th Year First Phase First Year Implementation Plan, approves the record without any objections. The following is a brief record of the province's plan: (1) "Report Before the Compilation of the Plan" In the 17th year, the province established the Provincial Compulsory Education Committee. In the 18th year, it conducted a survey of school-age children in the provincial capital, and 15 counties established Compulsory Education Committees. At the same time, the province directly established 160 primary schools to advocate for various counties. However, due to funding and local security reasons, few counties directly organized compulsory education, and many provincial and county primary schools were also closed. The existing schools are far from sufficient to accommodate the existing school-age children. Last year's Second National Education Conference has formulated a plan to promote compulsory education nationwide. The province has followed the order to adapt to the needs of school-age children and has referred to the actual situation of the local situation to formulate the First Year (19th year) Implementation Plan. It is divided into four phases with five years as one phase, taking August of the 19th year to July of the 24th year as the first phase, and formulated the First Phase Implementation Plan of Compulsory Education in Hubei Province. (2) "Preparations for Immediate Attention" At the beginning of this plan, the Provincial Compulsory Education Committee will first count the number of school-age children in the provincial capital that have been surveyed, and request the Education Department to urge all counties to establish Compulsory Education Committees. Those that have been established will be ordered to quickly organize surveys and statistics and formulate a school establishment plan. At the same time, expand the propaganda and promote the literacy movement so that the general public and education authorities can work together to ensure that all plans can be implemented step by step. (3) "Teacher Training Plan" From August of the 19th year to July of the 24th year, teacher training will be conducted in ten semesters, such as establishing provincial rural normal schools, rural teacher training institutes, adding compulsory education classes to women's normal schools, opening provincial normal colleges and attached special courses, opening teacher training correspondence departments, holding summer schools, opening private school teacher training classes, opening county rural normal schools, and holding various teacher registration, etc. (4) "Phased School Establishment Plan" There are four detailed measures for the province to directly organize schools (establishment of provincial compulsory education experimental zones and measures for adding classes in each phase). There are five detailed measures for counties to directly organize schools (establishment of county compulsory education experimental zones and plans for adding classes in counties with relatively affluent, sub-affluent, poor, and very poor funding). (5) "Preparation of School Building Plan" The sources of school buildings are divided into three types: borrowing, donation, and new construction. (6) "Fundraising Plan" First, the province will be fully responsible for the first year. From the second year onwards, the resolution of the National Education Conference will be presented to the central government to urge local authorities to implement it separately. Second, the province plans to handle the fundraising of compulsory education funds in various counties in two phases during these five years. In the first phase, the province will directly organize compulsory education in various counties. At the same time, counties that can directly organize will be given subsidies according to their quantity and achievements. In the later phase, the counties will directly organize completely. The Education Department may transfer the original provincial primary school buildings and school equipment to the county education bureau to manage the central primary school according to its performance and subsidize each county's compulsory education by 10% with provincial funds as decided by the National Education Conference. Third, regarding the methods for counties to directly raise compulsory education funds, in the first year and the second year, they will focus on reorganizing the original education funds and allocate 80% of the new income from the reorganization to compulsory education funds. From the third year onwards, counties that have not collected land tax should uniformly collect compulsory education land tax. Those who have collected land tax and used it for other purposes should fully allocate it to compulsory education funds. In the future, the county education bureau will propose additional production taxes or other surcharges based on the production in the area under its jurisdiction to increase funding. All of the funds will be used as the county's compulsory education funds. The procedures should be submitted by the county education bureau to the education department to consult with the finance department and report to the provincial government for implementation. (Omitted below)

The End of the City Scout Inspection 178

Capture of the Enemy General who Attacked the Camp

Prizes Awarded on Themed Names

The Shanghai City-wide Scout Inspection and Camporee has concluded. Council members are currently expediting the closing procedures. Various troops are also dispatching personnel to claim the prizes they earned. However, on the night of the fifth, dozens of students, including a Mr. Xiao from the Fudan High School, attempted to attack the camp. Fortunately, Deputy Commander Wang Gang commanded effectively and captured six spies on the spot, causing the enemy to retreat. This is a common occurrence during scout inspections, as the opposing side uses it to test the organizer's thoroughness in preparation and the depth of their resources. The details are recorded below for reference by those managing scout activities.

News of the Attack Arrives On the morning of the fifth, after the awards ceremony, scout troops from various schools began to depart and return to their schools. There were not many scouts left on the inspection grounds. At that time, the prizes were still displayed on the inspection platform. Deputy Commander Wang Gang, fearing a loss, assigned scouts to watch in shifts. Around 10 p.m., a report suddenly came in that dozens of students, led by a Mr. Wu and a Mr. Xiao, from the Fudan High School, were coming to attack the camp. He immediately issued an emergency order, instructing Security Chief Ni Jiaxi to increase the number of guard teams and diligently patrol. He also issued the password "Do One Good Deed a Day." Around 2 a.m., several dark figures headed straight for the defensive line. The security team questioned them for the password. Knowing that preparations had been made, the students attempted to flee, but female scouts bravely stepped forward and apprehended one person on the spot. Interrogation revealed that a large group of students was lurking around the perimeter. An order was issued for a thorough search, and Xiao, the leader of the vanguard, and five other members were captured. The enemy, finding the defenses too strong to penetrate, fled to the southern villages. At 3:30 a.m., the camp's management team organized a court, appointing Wang Gang, Shen Yu, and Dai Qiliu as military judges to conduct separate interrogations, which concluded at dawn. Later, Wu, the leader of the enemy, presented a certificate from the school requesting their release. After the military judges verified its authenticity, all were handed over to him to take away. The scout troop leaders, admiring the students' bravery in venturing out at night, honored them with a brief salute to show encouragement.

Prize Winners The prizes donated by various sectors, with the exception of the silver tripod donated by Chairman Chiang, which the council retained as a permanent memento, were awarded to the following: The Executive Yuan's silver shield was awarded to the 64th Troop; the Ministry of Military Affairs' silver shield was awarded to the 268th Troop; the Ministry of Navy's flag was awarded to the 7th Troop; the Ministry of Education's silver shield was awarded to the 177th Troop; the Ministry of Interior's silver shield was awarded to the 254th Troop; the Control Yuan's flag was awarded to the 14th Troop; the Training Directorate's flag was awarded to the 196th Troop; Song Ziwen's silver shield was awarded to the 20th Troop; Wang Zhengting's silver shield was awarded to the 268th Troop; Zhang Qun's silver cup was awarded to the 250th Troop; the rest are omitted for brevity.

Strong Rivals for Next Year's World Games 190

The Results of the Kanto Athletic Meet in Japan are Particularly Good 191

Three World Athletes Participated in Demonstrations, Nearly All Failed

200-Meter, Shot Put, and Discus Break Japanese Records

(Tokyo Correspondence) Japan, in preparation for next year's World Games, took the opportunity of holding the All-Kanto Athletic Meet to invite three world athletes from the United States and Switzerland to participate in demonstrations to learn from the techniques of the advanced athletes. The meet was organized by the Japan Athletic Association and held at the Meiji Jingu Stadium on April 25th and 26th. At the opening ceremony, Prince Chichibu, the Emperor's brother, came to the stage to give encouragement. On that day, due to the magical appeal of the three world athletes, tens of thousands of spectators came, creating an unprecedented scene. The most competitive events on the first day were the finals of the 100-meter, shot put, and 1500-meter races. The 100-meter race featured Simpson from the United States, while the main competitor from Japan was Yoshioka. During the semi-finals, Yoshioka's record of 10.7 seconds gave the American athlete a scare. However, before the finals, it was generally predicted that Yoshioka was no match for Simpson, as Simpson had a record of 10.3 seconds. Unexpectedly, Simpson was suppressed by Yoshioka in the finals, and the two reached the finish line at the same time, with a record of 10.7 seconds each. Yoshioka won first place by a chest length. In the 1500-meter final, the Swiss athlete, Marudan, competed against Japan's Tsuda. The two athletes stayed close to each other throughout the race, earning thunderous applause from the audience. Upon reaching the finish line, the Japanese athlete won by four meters, causing the world-renowned middle-distance runner to fail. In the shot put final, the American athlete, Loshan, participated. Loshan's usual record is 47-48 meters, but his performance this time was unexpectedly poor, failing to reach 40 meters throughout. The Japanese athletes, on the other hand, performed exceptionally well. The athlete, Hashibita, broke Saito's Japanese national record with a score of 43.17 meters. In addition, the results of the finals of the long jump, high jump, and 10,000-meter races were also very good. Overall, the three world athletes were completely defeated on the first day, showing that the progress of the Japanese is indeed threatening the world. As a result of the second day's competition, Simpson finally won the 200-meter final. Although the Japanese athletes, Yoshioka and Nakajima, were defeated in this event, they both broke the Japanese record one after another. Nakajima's score in the semi-finals was 21.3 seconds, and Yoshioka's score in the finals was 21.4 seconds. Simpson's score was 21 seconds, all of which are new records. Loshande also got his revenge in the shot put event. Because he was too tired, his first throw reached 14.31 meters, but his subsequent five throws were not good. However, no one could compete with him, and Takata Dayang, who held the Far East record, competed with him, but his score was only over 12 meters. The weakness of Easterners in throwing events was greatly exposed. The results of the two-day men's and women's competitions are recorded below.

Chu Minyi Requests Promotion of Tai Chi Exercises 193

Letter Sent to Four Central Training Department and Other Agencies

Tai Chi Exercises as a Literacy Movement in Physical Education

Central Committee Member Chu Minyi is very knowledgeable about physical education and hygiene and is very active in promoting it. In recent years, he has repeatedly stated that Tai Chi Quan is the most physiological exercise that cannot be achieved by general exercise methods. Therefore, he has spared no effort in promoting it. The number of scholars has gradually increased, and the effect is very significant. The physical education community, which has long been obsessed with Western exercise methods, has been refreshed by this. Mr. Chu is not satisfied with this. Because Tai Chi Quan is good, but it is not easy to popularize because its movements are complicated. It is not a book of physical exercise enlightenment. Teaching students to practice Tai Chi Quan is like teaching illiterate people to recite poetry and books. Therefore, he thinks day and night about how to improve it, taking the advantages of Tai Chi Quan and striving for simple movements to popularize it. Therefore, the invention of Tai Chi exercise originated. Mr. Chu was also afraid that it was not as satisfactory as people wanted, so he extensively consulted advanced figures in the physical education community and celebrities in the academic community to evaluate it. The result of the consultation was unanimous. They believe that it is the most rationalized exercise method, which is sufficient to be popularized throughout the country. It has hundreds of benefits and no disadvantages. Recently, he published all his works into a special book, divided into three steps and six sections, with diagrams and formulas. The description strives to be simple and the movements strive to be simple. Everything about the advantages and disadvantages, difficulties, ease, advantages and disadvantages of various movements, and the principles of physical education are described in detail. It has been printed by the Datong Bookstore and will soon be available to the world. Many people in all walks of life want to see it first. Mr. Chu also believes that the method of popularization will be slower if the government does not promote it. Yesterday, he sent letters to the Central Party Department, the Training Department, the Training Directorate, the Ministry of Education, and the Ministry of Internal Affairs, requesting them to actively promote it to promote public sports. The following is the draft of the letter (omitted above). As the European style has gradually spread eastward, our country, which has always been known for its weakness, has gradually paid attention to the strength of the nation and has engaged in physical exercise. In recent years, due to the active promotion of the central government, the public's interest has been strong, so there has been even more rapid development. From the surface, it is indeed a good phenomenon for the future of our nation, but a deeper investigation reveals many malpractices. Let us briefly discuss it. Now, those who talk about physical education must imitate Western methods and purchase all their equipment from foreign countries. A sports field cannot be built without tens of thousands of dollars, and a fitness room cannot be built without thousands of dollars. As for sports equipment and athletes' clothing, they often cost several dollars or more, and those that cost tens of dollars or hundreds of dollars are also common. This is the first point, which is not economical in terms of money. The exercise methods that are popular now require months of practice to become proficient. If you want to improve your skills, it takes years, even decades. This is the second point, which is not economical in terms of time. Today, those who can compete on the sports field must first have a strong physique to be competent. Because all sports are vigorous and require a lot of effort, even those with a strong physique will be out of breath and have palpitations after exercise. The old and weak can imagine the results. As a result, some get sick and some become disabled. This is the third point, which is not economical in terms of strength. If the actual harm is like this, why should we value exercise? The definition of exercise is simply to promote blood circulation and activate muscles and bones. The purpose of exercise is health. If a certain exercise can truly achieve the goal of health without any malpractices, then its methods can be transmitted from the West or from our country. Otherwise, we will not take it. In other words, we want to choose a perfect method to achieve its purpose. The malpractices of the various sports methods that are currently popular have been mentioned above, so we should resolutely abandon them and look for other ways. Therefore, Mr. Minyi, based on his experience of engaging in physical education for thirty years, has carefully studied the advantages and disadvantages, and suddenly realized that he invented Tai Chi exercise. Because its movements are all derived from Tai Chi Quan, it can also be called Tai Chi Quan-style exercise. Tai Chi Quan is the Taoist method in our country's martial arts. Its methods are beneficial and harmless, and it has been recognized by the whole country. However, its movements are frequent and difficult to remember. Therefore, it has been improved to be simple and become Tai Chi exercise, but it does not lose its original advantages. The advantages of Tai Chi exercise are three. First, it does not take time. It only takes a few minutes to complete a set of Tai Chi Quan exercises, which will not interfere with working hours. Second, it does not cost money. It only requires bare hand practice, whether indoors or outdoors, without equipment or decoration. You can practice it anywhere. Third, it does not take effort. Because Tai Chi exercise focuses on softness and peace, only seeking to promote blood circulation and activate muscles and bones to achieve the goal of health, it does not focus on danger and wonder to confuse people or brag about courage to impress the crowd. With these three major advantages, it is enough to surpass all other exercise methods. Our nation wants to have a healthy body, and we can only rely on this. Mr. Minyi has used this method to promote physical education and give demonstrations in Beijing, Shanghai, and other places, which have been highly praised by public opinion and sympathized by the academic community. It is considered to be harmless and sufficient to be popularized throughout the country to promote the nation. Recently, he began to write a special book, which includes a complete set of Tai Chi Quan, including everything, including the reasons for it, and a book of formulas and diagrams, and a hanging map of formulas. He has entrusted the Shanghai Datong Bookstore to print it. The volume is headed by Mr. Li Shizeng, Liu Shangqing, Zhang Yuejun, Zhang Zhijiang, Xiao Mengsheng, and Xu Zhiyi, who have written prefaces based on their experience in practicing Tai Chi Quan or based on the method of Tai Chi exercise, praising it as a creation of the physical education community. The publication of the book is not far away. Your department, which leads the group and develops physical education, will definitely be doubled by Mr. Minyi. In addition to asking for review after the book is published, I will first attach a draft of the first part of the complete Tai Chi exercise book. If you are willing to adopt it and think that it is feasible, please strongly promote it to save the day and strengthen the nation.

The Completion of the North China Venue is Near 194

The Shandong Provincial Games Opens Today

Jinan Correspondence The entire project of the North China Games venue is only half a month away from the scheduled completion date. Currently, it is working hard. There are more than 1,300 workers in total. Today (4th), the weather was cloudy and rainy, and the work did not stop. The field event venues, such as the shot put and discus positions, and the long jump and high jump square pools, have been set up. The cinder track is paved with sand, which is very smooth. Shang Shumei, Zhang Yixian, Guo Shiying, and others measured and buried the starting and finishing wooden signs in the rain today. The construction of the grandstand has reached the ninth level on the south and west sides, and the sixth level on the east side. The rain shelter is also 70-80% complete. The north-facing rostrum is being built on the foundation, and beams and columns are being erected. It will be completed soon, but it will not be available for the Provincial Games. A temporary rostrum is being built on the east side, which will be completed tomorrow. The external construction of the new office building has also been completed, and the interior walls are being decorated. The North China Preparatory Committee will soon be able to move in to work. After the closing of the North China Games, it will be used as the office for the Shandong Provincial Public Sports Field. The Shandong Provincial Games is scheduled to be held from the 7th to the 10th. The day before the opening ceremony (5th), all instructors will gather at the Public Cinema in the city to first study all the matters of the Games. The groups and schools participating in the Provincial Games are continuing to register.

Also, the North China Preparatory Committee has recently received a batch of prizes. Zhang Jiancun, a member of the Shandong Provincial Rectification Committee, donated a silver shield with the inscription "Pioneer for the People." A Word of Insight 195

— Xing Mu

"Tomorrow" is the word that most relaxes people's minds. How many "tomorrows" can one have in a lifetime? Many ambitious people are misled by the thought of "tomorrow." Therefore, Western philosophers say, "Do not leave today's work for tomorrow." This is a true saying.

Love is originally a comedy, but it is precisely because of its comedy that it is interesting. If you take it too seriously, the result of love is only pain.

Those who labor with their minds eat what their minds labor for, and those who labor with their bodies eat what their bodies labor for. "Who knows that every grain on the plate is hard-earned?" This saying was originally sung for farmers, but if you savor it carefully, people all over the world should think like this.

Prostitutes sell their smiles in a tangible way, while literati sell their smiles in an intangible way. Xu Zhuodai compared himself to someone leaning against the door when he compiled the "Smiling Paintings," which is very meaningful.

Lin Pinqing spent her entire life only paying off debts with tears. In fact, who in the world is not like this? Only tears have a heart. The tears in the heart are even more painful than the tears in the eyes.

People have infatuation, favoritism, respect, and affection for their wives. The result of infatuation and favoritism is the Ji Chang addiction in the world. Those who want to enjoy true happiness in the boudoir, why not change infatuation to respect and shift favoritism to affection?

A Record of the Self-Defense Corps of Xiaxi Village, Fenghua 196

— Tang Bing'an

There is a village called Xiaxi in the mountains of Fenghua, about a hundred miles away from the county seat. It is adjacent to Xinchang and is a place where bandits often appear. Nearby villages have been burned and looted. Those who pass through the area, if they do not prepare in advance, will be taken advantage of by these bandits. They may rob property or kidnap people. The ransom for the kidnapped does not necessarily have to be wealthy, and the ransom price can be as low as tens of dollars, unlike the kidnapping in Shanghai, where the price is often tens of thousands of dollars. Xiaxi Village is located in the bandit area. With the help of the self-defense corps, it is the only village that can be completely preserved. The village is surrounded by mountains, and the terrain is very dangerous. The Dong family is the largest family. Dong Huating and his brothers are well-fed and are skilled in shooting. They can hit flying birds with 100% accuracy. For a time, they were known as "Flying Guns." Seeing the prevalence of banditry, he warned his clan members, "Born in a time of turmoil, bandits are rampant. Our village is far from the city, and the military and police cannot reach it. It is especially easy for bandits to covet. We must take precautions. Now, I agree with the elders and brothers in the village that all young adults in the village should learn shooting. Women should also engage in this after managing household affairs. Then, once a disaster occurs, we can be prepared." Everyone said it was good. Huating donated money to purchase weapons and established a self-defense corps. When the corps members are not busy, they farm. When something happens, they are temporarily summoned. Huating and his brothers serve as coaches. Huating also assessed the terrain of the village, where to defend and where to attack. The planning is detailed and organized. After a long time, it became an elite force. At first, the bandits thought that Xiaxi Village was small and easy to start. One night, they came to rob the village with torches. Huating learned of this in advance and gathered dozens of strong men to ambush on the main road, waiting with live ammunition. The bandits did not know and led the team to advance, many of whom were ambushed and killed. Therefore, they fled in droves. From then on, the bandits warned each other not to dare to commit crimes. In the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, a group of bandits called Thousands of People planned to rob a certain village, but they had to pass through Xiaxi. They sent messengers to Huating in advance to ask for permission to pass. They also said that if he did not allow them, they would first rob Xiaxi Village. Huating did not move. Dozens of bandits came with whips and then left. Therefore, the bandits hated Huating and his brothers to the bone and offered 5,000 dollars to buy Huating and his brothers. They were so feared by the bandits. When the Northern Expeditionary Army arrived in Jiangzhe, our remaining warlords in Yong heard the news and led their troops to flee. Wherever they passed, they set fires and robbed chickens and dogs, but they finally did not dare to touch Xiaxi Village. This is also strange. Huating is skilled in shooting, and his wife and daughter are also experts in their own right, with every bullet hitting the target. His son, Zhenhan, followed my brother-in-law, Le Bin, to travel, so I learned the details. I hereby record it to enrich this discussion and tell the world those who are running the security corps.

A PAGE OF LAUGHTER AND TEARS FROM HISTORY 201

— Ms. Yeh Hua

It has been a long time since Chaplin acted in a circus, three years to be exact. Three years ago, a German reporter allowed the American leftist writer Sinclair to interview Chaplin. Sinclair returned home and wrote an article about Chaplin's writing, directing, and starring in the production of "City Lights." He said that Chaplin worked hard day and night. After the film was completed, it was destroyed because it was not satisfactory, and then re-shot. This happened countless times. The article was reprinted in the magazine Living Age, November 1929. In the same year, my younger brother Lingfeng translated it into Chinese. This highly anticipated masterpiece is now premiering in Shanghai in this season of new green willows and blooming peach and plum blossoms.

I once said that the biggest problem in life is to not see the true state of the world. It is clearly a society of male thieves and female prostitutes, but it is still called a land of sages and propriety. Chaplin, on the screen, can make people carefully examine contemporary society. In the vastness of life, he often grasps segments of life and uses artistic techniques to imply their meaning. His works are not only expressions of life but also interpretations of life. Chaplin is a comedian but also a tragedian. His background is full of heartbreaking sights and is full of blood and tears. Watching this play further strengthens the belief that the rich in the play are like two different people when awake and drunk. This is a depiction of dual personalities. The formation of dual personalities is due to the functions of the unconscious and conscious mind, and it is also the general pivot of good and evil. It is not an exaggeration to say that a person's life is a history of the conflict of dual personalities. The fact that the tramp is imprisoned for saving a woman proves that crime has meaning and injustice. The wealthy create poverty, and the law cannot guarantee human rights. This makes people feel a sense of resentment towards the concept of rewarding and punishing. The tramp struggles with fate and is innocently humiliated, which is like speaking out against injustice for ordinary people. The whole play cannot escape love because "love" is the essence of life and the vitality of new life. Loving a lonely blind friend is deeply meaningful. If the ending is a broken heart, it can show the world's ingratitude and the fact that love is truly blind. However, the fact that it ends happily is why this comedy is called a comedy. The film is silent but plays sound music. The lighting throughout the film is black, gray, and white, fully revealing the nature of photography. It is similar to Chaplin's "A Woman of Paris." Aside from the dance hall, there are only two or three people in the film. Chaplin is still wearing his old clothes, the eighteen-year-old rubber New York actor's specially made mustache is still intact. I felt endlessly moved while watching this film. Compared to those who have hundreds of legs dancing in unison, with the aroma of meat filling the air, and who sing love songs without thinking while walking and dancing, the difference is immeasurable.

THE FATED LOVE AFFAIR AND A NOVEL MODEL 202

— Cheng Tanglu

In recent years, there have been many people who have studied novels with me, but they have been troubled by the lack of a novel model to help them learn by analogy. Since Zhang Henshui's "The Fated Love Affair" caused a sensation and broke the records of previous novelists, the excellent structure and skillful descriptions in the book are obvious to all and need no further explanation. However, it is difficult to find a good novel, and it is even more difficult to find a good critic of a novel. "Dream of the Red Chamber" is certainly excellent, but the critics of "Dream of the Red Chamber" are all mediocre and unable to enhance the book's brilliance. "The Fated Love Affair" is famous because of Zhang Henshui's wonderful writing, and it is even more famous because of Duhe's wonderful commentary. Although Duhe only wrote a preface, the preface is very long and reveals the methods of writing "The Fated Love Affair" and the essence of the book. It can be regarded as a general commentary that complements the book perfectly. It is truly a wonderful story in the garden of literature. Whenever students ask me about the methods of writing novels, I always say, "Why don't you buy "The Fated Love Affair" as a novel model? It has Zhang Henshui's wonderful writing and Duhe's wonderful commentary. "The embroidered mandarin ducks are there for you to see" is Zhang Henshui's work, and "handing the golden needle to others" is Duhe's commentary. The students, upon hearing my words, each bought a copy of "The Fated Love Affair" and studied it carefully. As a result, their thinking and writing skills improved day by day. They thanked me for my guidance. I said, "You don't need to thank me, you should thank Zhang Henshui, and especially thank Duhe, who commented on Zhang Henshui's work."

THE OLD CAPITAL IN SPRING 203

— Jiguan

My old friend Mr. Yu Yue came south from Pingjin yesterday and told me about the latest news from the old capital. Feeling bored by the sunny window, I picked up my pen and wrote about it.

Since the government established its capital in Nanjing, the spring scenery of the old capital has changed greatly. Although dance halls have been opened and female attendants have been widely used in recent years, the markets are deserted and all industries remain depressed. This is why the general people of Beiping are frowning and sighing. The call for a prosperous Ping city is very high. Until last month, when Zhang Xueliang organized the Deputy Commander's Office in Ping, the majority of citizens began to feel that there was hope for realizing prosperity. They were excited and colorful, and the market situation was revitalized, which was truly unprecedented in the past few years.

Famous restaurants in Beiping, such as Dalu Chun and Tongchun Yuan, are located on Chang'an Street, no fewer than ten or so. Their usual business is desolate. During Zhang Xueliang's presence in Ping, they were crowded with customers every day. The archways in the Qianmen area are tall and the electric lights are bright at night, attracting many tourists. The major silk shops took this opportunity to reduce prices and attract customers, which was also very profitable. Other industries, such as theaters and amusement parks, also saw an increase in revenue. Mr. Chu Minyi even took the stage to perform a crosstalk in Hualeyuan, performing an excerpt from "The Weishui River". That evening, Zhang Xueliang specifically booked several boxes to invite guests to enjoy the performance. Important figures such as Hu Ruoyu and Yu Xuezhong all came together, beaming with joy and celebrating peace in the bright spring, adding color to the Ping market.

TRAVELS IN INDIA (45) 204

— Linghua

On February 1st, I attended a meeting with Ms. La Haoying, Fei Libu, Keli, Swiss Ms. Hoy, Mrs. Phillips Currie Holz, Zedi, the president of the La Haoying Student Union, and Zhendixin, the secretary of the hall. Ms. Hoy, a young Swiss woman in her early twenties, said that the Swiss did not understand the meaning of war. Fei Libu said that male politics is the root of war. The government collects our taxes, turning our money and property into guns and cannons, and even conscripts our lives as tools of masculinity. I only have one son who is seventeen years old this year. I don't know when a major war will suddenly break out, and my son's life will not be guaranteed. Ms. Keli said that her friend, Ms. Meili's first husband died in the war, and her second husband also died in the war. Now she has married her third husband with great difficulty, and she is very afraid every time she hears of war. In the past, Rome had a proverb that Roman men managed all the men in the world, and the wives of Roman men managed our husbands. However, their management was not good, only allowing the Roman heroes to slaughter the world. In the future, we should change to a good law to teach children not to learn to fight and kill. Student Union President Jai Dev held a letter questioning, roughly saying that the root of world wars is still material. Generally, he based his arguments on Marxist academic theory, because many young people in India now know Marx. Fei Libu said that her family had a mother cat who gave birth to four kittens. One day, the mother cat went out and all the kittens were bitten to death by male cats, and their intestines were broken open, but they were not eaten. From this observation, the male's nature is to kill the offspring of the female, which has nothing to do with Marx. The male old cat kills the kittens without eating them, which is no different from the massacre of a city by a great robber. Genghis Khan and Napoleon were also great male cats. I don't fully believe in Marx's words. Ms. Keli said that her family had two hens and three roosters. Each of the two hens brought more than ten chicks to forage for food separately without fighting. The roosters had no burden of chicks and easily fought when they met, which proves that fighting is not necessarily related to the problem of bread. Ms. Keli said that everyone knows if the future war starts from which country? Everyone did not answer her. She said that she was afraid that England and the United States would compete for dominance. As a result, Ms. Fei Libu was appointed as an organizing committee member of La Haoying City.

On the 2nd, Ms. Keli and her daughter came to Fei Libu's house. Fei Libu said that Ms. Keli was a leader among British women with knowledge and profound academic skills. She asked me many questions that were related to explaining that she had seen four ducklings hatched by a hen in the garden. I asked her why she had let the hen hatch ducks. She said that she had chicken eggs, but after hatching, only ducks were left. The hen loved the ducks as if they were her own, without any discrimination. When an eagle and dog looked down, the hen made an angry shape to protect the ducklings. This matter is very interesting and can prove that the maternal rights of animals protect their offspring not only by protecting their own offspring but also by protecting what they raise. Now the male system is killing each other because the mothers only know how to raise them, but do not know how to protect their offspring rights. I thought that her observation of animals was very philosophical. This matter was once considered a major issue by Goethe and his friend, a certain great biologist, because one day Goethe's friend saw a wren bird being raised in a robin's nest. The friend told Goethe, and the two used this example to say that it was a great invention of animal socialism. Animals can truly unconsciously implement the principles of not only loving their own parents but also loving their own children, which is far superior to humans. Now, Ms. Fei Libu has also paid attention to this.

Because of this thought, my attitude calmed down instead, and I said to him again, "There is a twist here that you haven't understood yet. The person who ran away is the real culprit. GOLD PRICE DROPS BY FIVE TAELS 207

Opens Flat, Plunges at Noon

Trading Among Firms Still Lacks Large Volumes

Yesterday, the 6th, the gold price once again showed a downward trend, with the weight already testing the 740 tael level. The situation within the customs was very flat, with fluctuations of only one or two taels. However, from morning to noon, there was a total of more than seven taels of difference. Looking back, it ended up falling five taels again. The selling sentiment among firms was very strong. It was still firm in the early morning, but almost as soon as the overseas silver market rose and fell differently, there was a slight shrinkage and hovering around 41 taels. Because the official and unofficial exchange rates were both flat, suddenly at noon there was a flood of looseness, and the stable market was turned into fatigue by the sellers. There was a sharp drop of seven taels, and the situation was soft. Finally, it only counted 36 taels. In the afternoon, because it was the spring racing season, the market was still closed. In the early morning, the June opening rose by one tael to 742 taels, followed by two taels and five cents. The price for large bars suddenly rose by sixteen-one-hundredths, and the silver price was reduced by eight-one-hundredths. Private telegraphs were the same, and because the United States sold out, people's hearts were high. Afterwards, because Yu Dafeng and Yongfeng and others sold, the price fell by one tael. At 9:00, the British gold announcement was unchanged, only the East Exchange hung up at 25, but it was not moved, and it had fallen to 40 taels. After entering the bank, the bank ate up 375 British gold, and in addition, Yuan Maoyong, Fuyu and Hedging and others bought in, gradually moving forward. At 9:50, it rose to 42 taels and 9 cents. Afterwards, Yuan Cheng and Yongheng and others sold out, slightly less than one tael and zero. At 10:10, it was 41 taels and 6 cents, and after a quarter of an hour, it added one tael to two taels and five cents. Because Gan Changxiang, Heng Yu Dada, and Desheng sold, it fell by more than one tael. At 10:45, it was 41 taels, and suddenly Hengxing came to buy. Also, Taiwan absorbed 375 British gold in August, so it increased by one tael. At 11:10, it was 42 taels and 4 cents. After that, it showed a downward trend. Yongfeng had a strong desire to sell, and the numbers followed suit, and the momentum was unstoppable. The market sentiment was agitated, and it continued to fall by four or five taels. SILVER DOLLAR MARKET IS FIRM, SOFT, AND UNEVEN 210

Flour Market Strengthens Due to Rain 216

Yesterday, the flour market opened in the morning, and conditions in each month were generally stable. Although imported wheat quotations were better by one or two jiao, the weather was still good. Both buyers and sellers saw little special progress, and the market remained stable, with minimal activity. However, after the afternoon opening, heavy rain and the prospect of prolonged rainfall raised concerns about wheat, even though the harvest was still far away. This caused sentiment to turn positive and buying interest to gradually increase, with prices for each month rising by about one fen. The situation should ease if the weather turns clear. As a result, May and June rose one fen compared to the previous day, July rose seven and a half li, August rose five li, September rose one fen, and October rose five li.

Wheat Market Trends Towards Stability Again 217

Yesterday, the futures wheat market saw a trend towards stability in various months during both the morning and afternoon sessions. Better quotations for imported wheat and excessive rainfall also made inland sentiment stable. Additionally, domestic bankruptcies led to limited buying of distant futures. As imported wheat was not suitable and there was uncertainty about the domestic wheat harvest, more observed, and fewer sold, so market sentiment gradually strengthened. As a result, the current month was up two fen compared to the previous day, June was up two fen, and July to October were all up three fen.

Sericulture: Jinhua Early Silkworms are Asleep, Leaves are Flourishing 220

Unfortunately, Continuous Wind and Rain... Silkworms Eat Wet Leaves and Excrete Yellow

Farmers in the old Jinhua Prefecture of Zhejiang Province generally start raising silkworms during the Qingming Festival, but due to the cold weather, they delayed until after the Grain Rain Festival to start collecting ants, and the number of ants hatched was only about 70%. After the leaves came out, the weather was not warm and spring rain fell frequently, which was not conducive to the development of silkworms. Farmers and instructors felt very difficult to care for them. In several places, white stiff early silkworms have been found and are now asleep with flourishing leaves. However, due to continuous strong winds and heavy rain, the silkworms eat more leaves. The wet leaves that are collected cannot be dried in time, resulting in the silkworms eating wet leaves and excreting yellow water. Silkworm farmers are generally worried.

Qimen Tea Prices are Difficult to Lower 221

Qimen new black tea has officially opened for weighing for a week. The price of high-grade tea from Xilu Zhuang boat plate is above 100 yuan. The price of tender tip tea from Ti Zhuang is 140 to 150 yuan. The price of goods from Nanlu and Fuzhuang has also opened to 80 yuan. Before the Grain Rain, the price of young bud leaves was 600,000 cash copper coins per dan, which is equivalent to more than 200 silver dollars, which is the highest price ever. At the beginning of the opening of each tea shop, the intention for this year's mountain price was to generally reduce it as before, but they knew that the situation of the new tea on the market had changed. In order to rush to get new tea, the industry could not wait and immediately opened the price according to the price. The cautious tea shops knew that the cost was too high and they would be in danger, but because the situation had become a tiger riding, they could not stop and had to follow the price to do a little. Recently, the top-quality goods from high-grade tea plantations in the Jiajia River area of ​​Qixi have been shipping quite well, and the production method is also excellent. Qi · Shining Star · Gaotang · Hengshunxiang and other tea shops are all concentrated there to search for tea, and the price is difficult to lower. The opening and output prices of Baojia Cen · Ya Hang · Pancun roads in recent days still require 80 to 70 yuan. Yesterday and today, the weather was suddenly rainy and suddenly sunny, and the quality of the leaves was not soaked in the morning dew. The shipment will be easier and more inferior. The tea houses are to protect their capital, and they do not care about adding to the mountain households this time. The households are always few tea and many numbers, and they are not worried about backlog. It is still difficult to reduce the price.

Yujiang New Tea is Being Picked 222

Yujiang (ie Anren) is an important tea-producing area in eastern Jiangxi. The tea is delicate and tender, and is favored by tea shops. However, the aroma is less than that of Wu tea. This year, the climate is turning early, and the head tea of ​​each mountain garden is being picked. In recent days, half of the mountain households have opened their gardens. Although a small number of tea shop customers from Nanchang and Kou are in the mountains to search, the output price is not high. The mountain households have made it ready and are waiting for foreign tea shops to open and then give the price.

Wuchang Tea Picking and Production Affected by Rainy Weather 223

The head tea in Wuyuan has been produced in unison for several days, but because the development of late tea is slow, it cannot be picked at the same time. The tea buds have been longer in the past two days, and they are being picked and roasted. Also, because the weather is rainy and there is no morning dew, the aroma is slightly worse. It takes time and effort to stir-fry the leaves and knead the blanks, and the amount of harvest is also less than that in sunny weather. Therefore, the tea picking and production work of mountain households has been greatly affected by the rainy weather.

Guoshan Yunwu Tea Has Shown Its Tips 224

Zhangshan Yunwu Tea is the highest treasure among foreign green teas. The quality of water, leaves, and aroma is unparalleled in the world. The tea trees in the mountains are in high positions and the climate is cold and less warm. The tea buds develop later than in other places. According to mountain households, the climate this year is also turning early, and the tea trees have shown white hairs and small tips. It can be picked after the tea in each continent has been picked.

Art World

After Seeing the Morning Light Exhibition 228

— Yun

At dawn, the birds in the graveyard next door were singing very energetically, as if intentionally calling me awake from my sleep.

Deep in my mind was the thought that I would never forget: to visit the Morning Light Fifth Art Exhibition. "Good, go early!" I actually shouted, and the joyful mood was self-evident. But why would it make me so happy? At least I believe that this exhibition will not disappoint me, and I have considerable confidence in it. Especially the works of several strong newcomers have long been eagerly awaited by me, and I want to see what they are like. On the bus, gusts of light breeze brushed around me. I was really fascinated by the morning light, making my heart active. I don't know where the life experiences and various thoughts flew to, but the expression on my face was just an unstoppable smile.

After a long time, the Morning Light venue was stepped on by me. One painting after another appeared before my eyes. They were all full of life, as if they were acting, leading me into the world. Needless to say, their protagonists could cry sadly, but there were also very high-spirited ones, telling me that the future of the nation is bright and limitless as long as we work hard.

Now let me talk casually about my two-hour impression there on the works of old and new writers.

Among the watercolor works, the works of Mr. Song Zhiqin and Mr. Yang Taiyang can be said to be the best in terms of skills. Mr. Song is better with several sketches, such as "Stream Tree", "Village", "Spring Field", etc., all of which can be considerate and detailed, and there is no clumsy place. It can be called a successful work. Mr. Yang's "Morning Park" is a feature. Although it is a small piece, the light and vigorous brushwork, the proper color matching, and the harmony of the air are definitely not something that a high-talent person can have.

Ms. Guan Zilan's paintings are making rapid progress. This time, there are "Portrait" (self-portrait), "Girl", "Still Life", "Flower", etc. Among them, "Still Life" is the best. How much higher is the interest of an apple in the eyes of an appraiser than eating a real apple?

Mr. Chen Baoyi, an old writer who is most famous for his sketch oil paintings, has about ten works this time, all of which show his unique experience. Anyone who has seen his paintings will know that Mr. Chen has reached the pinnacle, such as "After Spring Rain" and "Lake Scenery". I want to wonder how he can describe it. How wonderful is that mountain that makes people drunk? What's more, there is that gorgeous lake water. I have no words to describe it, just say it is mysterious. "Yan Zhi's Sketch" and "Yellow Leaves" are all great. I think Mr. Chen is on par with Mr. Kawagita Kiyoyone and other Japanese painters.

Although Mr. Wang Daoyuan only has one "Racecourse" this time, his painting skills will of course make people recognize it, and I don't need to go into details. You can also see this illustration in the newly published "Pioneer Monthly". The colors are very harmonious and bright.

The works of Mr. Huang Zhenzhong and Mr. Xu Suling are also eye-catching. Mr. Huang's "Miss Ma Lan" is slightly inferior. "Impression of Changsha" takes the suffering of the disaster area as the subject matter and paints the terrifying state of inhumanity. Several lying corpses are set off by the red light of the fire in the distance. At this time, we can imagine the panic of the people in the environment from this picture. Mr. Xu's "Nocturne" can be called a masterpiece. It depicts several friends wandering on the street singing wildly in search of a place to stay. Can a sad person not sympathize with them?

In addition, the "Lakeside" by Fang Ganmin, the "Port of Zhenhai" by Chen Qiucao, the "Twilight" by Du Xueou, and the "Summer of Qingdao" by Pan Sitong all have their own strengths and are more exciting than their previous works.

There are also several writers, such as Weng Yuanchun and Lu Xiaoxia, whose works have their own advantages. I will not go into details one by one.

In short, this exhibition can satisfy the audience in terms of both quality and quantity, and at the same time, it has indeed gained a lot of hints...

Finally, what I want to say is that "in the current era of change, no nation is not struggling and fighting in the competition for survival." Several writers who want to work hard for nationalistic art will surely continue to do so seriously to "promote the nation's will to develop upward in order to form a new life for the nation." I think everyone longs for this. In fact, it is shouldering the greatest mission of art.

It is expected that there will be many new offerings at that time.

Kefa Pharmacy at No. 120 Nanjing Road announced that the weather has been abnormal recently, suddenly cold, suddenly warm, sometimes sunny, sometimes rainy. If you are not careful, you are prone to illness, and cough is especially common. According to the cough injury lung, the lung is one of the most important parts of the human body. If the cough is not treated, it often becomes pneumonia, tuberculosis, etc. A type of "Que Ke" medicine produced by this pharmacy specializes in treating coughs and has the effect of removing diseases. Purchasers have praised it endlessly.

Publishing News 231

Liming Bookstore is organized by people in the educational circles of this port. In recent years, it has published very exciting books. For example, the outline of social science and learning edited by Sun Hanshui, Yang Yinpu's "Yang's Chinese Finance Theory," Zhu Binyuan's "Money and Banking Theory," and Zhang Zhi's "Land Economics," etc., are all famous works that have been praised for a while. Sales are all over three or four editions. Recently, the bureau has set up a general distribution office in Huazhong Bookstore at the intersection of Wangping Street, Zhongshi Road, Simadu, in this port because of the need for business development to set up a store. From April 25th, it will hold a big cheap event jointly with Bizhong Bookstore for one month. Various books are cheaper than the usual prices.

Youth Garden

Fudan and Zhonggong Basketball Game 232

— Yu Xi

That day (April 29), we watched the Fudan and Zhonggong basketball competition.

The Fudan team came by car. The players and attendants, together with the cheerleaders, filled three cars. Many female players also came. They were like flowers walking across the playground, which was very attractive. Therefore, there were really a lot of people watching the game that day. All the students of Zhonggong were dispatched, surrounding the small East playground heavily.

Long benches were placed around the court. After the benches were occupied, the later spectators were blocked by the bench railings, and no matter how hard they tried to squeeze in, they could not cross the boundary line. This is the most effortless way to Kkeep line with the audience. I hope that large-scale football games will also use this method to save the flag-wavers from having a hard time chasing the spectators.

The women's friendly match was held first. Fudan players such as Chen Dinghe, He Emei, and Li Lian were all strong women's basketball players. Their heights were taller than those of the Zhonggong team (half of the Zhonggong team were squatty fat men), and their skills were more advanced than those of Zhonggong. Therefore, the result of six to twelve seemed not unexpected.

However, there are also outstanding roles in the Zhonggong team. For example, Zhang Zhaohe is a very promising player. All the six points scored by Zhonggong were thrown by her alone. Of course, she was the most limelight in this competition.

However, the more limelight, the more suffering she suffered. When Miss Zhang was playing vigorously, she slipped and fell to the ground. The rain was wet and the clothes were stained with mud. Everyone laughed, but it is a sign of bravery to fall while playing. There is really no reason to laugh.

But the spectators' unreasonableness is more than this.

For example, when they were holding the ball and throwing it into the blue, the men would shout in a woman's voice Shoo—What does this mean? Also, when the referee has a slightly inappropriate place, they will hiss or call. That is even more pointless.

We spectators can only watch and cannot interfere with the "administration" on the field. It is appropriate to clap your hands or yell a few times to encourage them at the appropriate time. Strange shouts like hooligans making trouble in the theater are out of line.

The Fudan team was led by their sports instructor. The sports instructor is often called "monster" by others. That day, he was wearing a raincoat, a bird-hunting hat on his head, and long black leather boots on his feet. His complexion was the complexion of an American Indian, and his eyebrows were always locked as if he was very sad.

In fact, he was very proud at that time because Fudan was winning.

When the women's basketball stopped, he squatted in front of the female players, making gestures to teach them all kinds of thresholds to defeat the enemy. From a distance, it looked like a mute was kneeling and proposing. The spectators hissed at him and turned around to look around, neither smiling nor scolding, and turned back to continue his Lecture.

"Peter" is always famous for his thick skin, but if you are a physical education teacher, you must have a thick skin, especially if you are a female physical education instructor. Thick skin is an indispensable condition. For example, Liu Liang, who is in our school, is really not young. That day, he was the timer for the men's game. Usually, he would blow the whistle after Haf-tim was over, but he was whimsical and fired a gun, scaring the spectators near him to jump.

In the men's game, Zhonggong won first, and finally Fudan turned defeat into victory, creating a ratio of twenty to twenty-six.

In terms of skills, men are of course much better than women. However, there are also shortcomings in the beauty. Some players often stop for a long time when they catch the ball, without moving forward or dispatching. The opponent does not come forward to snatch it, but just waits for the ball to be released. This kind of "calm" play, although not against the rules, loses a lot of excitement and wastes time. It is not economical. This is my layman's criticism. If there is anything wrong, I hope that you who have studied sports will give me advice.
